    WHEN CAST(LEN([l].[tenlaptop]) AS int) > 20 THEN COALESCE(SUBSTRING([l].[tenlaptop], 0 + 1, 20), N'') + N'...'

    SELECT TOP(1) [d].[madon], [d].[PhuongThucThanhToan], [d].[gia], [d].[giaohang], [d].[makh], [d].[ngaydat], [d].[ngaygiao], [d].[thanhtoan], [d].[tinhtrang]
    FROM [DonHang] AS [d]
    WHERE [d].[makh] = @__userId_0 AND [d].[tinhtrang] = 'CART'
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [ChiTietDonHang] AS [c] ON [t].[madon] = [c].[madon]
ORDER BY [t].[madon], [c].[madon]

    SELECT [c].[madon], [c].[malaptop], [c].[dongia], [c].[gia], [c].[soluong], [l].[malaptop] AS [malaptop0], [l].[cpu], [l].[giaban], [l].[gpu], [l].[hardware], [l].[hinh], [l].[mahang], [l].[manhinh], [l].[manhucau], [l].[mota], [l].[ngaycapnhat], [l].[pin], [l].[ram], [l].[soluongton], [l].[tenlaptop], [l].[trangthai]
